    <section class="core-section-container
        core-section-container--with-border border-b-1 border-solid border-color-border-faint py-4 text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us">
<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Etgi Grup; eğitim teknolojileri ve video konferans yazılımları konusunda yenilikçi ARGE kuruluşudur.

ETGi Grup dünyaca ünlü birçok teknoloji devinin Türkiye temsilciliğini yapıyor ve satış, eğitim, destek hizmetleri sunuyor.

ETGi Grup, müşterilerininin Türkiye ve yurtdışı projelerinde deneyimli ekipleri ve dünyaca ünlü iş ortakları ile her türlü  danışmanlık ve destek hizmetleri
ve çözümler sağlıyor.                  

Etgi Grup Zoom Video konferans yazılımlarının Türkiye'deki ilk partneridir. 
Video konferans, webinar ve bütünleşik iletişim ihtiyaçları için  satış, destek ve eğitim sunmaktadır. Etgi Grup, Zoom konusunda yüzlerce kurumsal müşteriye hizmet veriyor.

Video konferans donanım  ihtiyaçları için Logitech, ViewSonic, Jabra, Wacom, Polycom, Telycam, MXL, Yamaha, Insta360 VR gibi ürünler sunuyor.  

ETGi Grup video içerik oluşturulması, sunumu (stream) ve yönetimi içinde Vimeo ürünlerini müşterilerine sunuyor. 

Video, animasyon, etkileşimli içerik, VR/AR dijital içerik geliştirme araçları olarak ise ETGi Grup'un sağladığı ürünler
Techsmith Camtasia, Snagit, Articulate, Articulate 360, Rise, Vyond, Powtoon, 3D Video Plotagon, iSpring,  e-Learning Brothers Lectora,
CenarioVR, Adobe Creative Suite, FlippingBook ve Manycam. 

Ayrıca ETGi Grup online eğitim, iletişim ve uzaktan çalışma ihtiyaçları için Vedubox i geliştirdi. 
Vedubox yüzlerce müşteri tarafından kullanılıyor ve  binlerce kullanıcıya hizmet veriyor.
Vedubox bayi, personel, müşteri eğitimleri, ürün tanıtım ve demoları, etkinlikleri için gelişmiş entegre bir sistem sunuyor. Eğitim kurumları, kurslar ve okullar tarafından da kullanılıyor.
Kuruma özel bir portal olarak kullanılıyor. 
Vedubox online eğitim sistemi, LMS, e-ticaret sistemi, online sınav sistemi, üyelik sistemi, haber, duyuru, sms, email iletişim sistemi özelliklerini içinde bulunduruyor.
Toplantı, etkinlik ve online canlı eğitimler için Zoom, Google Meet gibi ürünler Vedubox içinde entegre bir modül olarak sunuluyor.
          </p>

İşte tam da burada <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fzoomworkplace&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#ZoomWorkplace</a> + <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Faicompanion&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AICompanion</a> devreye giriyor. 🚀

✅ <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fyapayzeka&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Yapayzeka</a>, toplantıları özetliyor, görevleri önceliklendiriyor,

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🚀 A major innovation at <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fzoomtopia&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Zoomtopia</a>: <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Faicompanion&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AICompanion</a> 3.0!

Zoom is transforming the way we work not only in meetings, but also across chat, email, calendar, and documents.

One of the most exciting features: AI-enhanced notes. This powerful feature, which expands our memory and productivity, is supported by the highest quality transcription, summarization, and translation thanks to Zoom's Federated AI infrastructure.

✨ Highlights:
* AI Companion is now an app → A personal hub for productivity and collaboration.
* Cross-platform support → Recognizes your Google or Microsoft email, calendar, and documents, helping you wherever you spend your time, including Slack and Teams.
* New “Agent-to-Agent Protocol” → Orchestrates external agents like ServiceNow within AI Companion and agents on other platforms like Google Agentspace and Salesforce Agentforce.
* Support throughout the entire meeting lifecycle → Planning, agenda, note-taking, summarizing, reporting, writing assistance, and proactive notifications.

Zoom-style: higher quality, lower cost, more secure! 💡

              <span class="!text-xs text-color-text-low-emphasis leading-[1.33333] px-0.25 flex">

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="feed-reshare-content__commentary">We launched AI Companion 3.0 at Zoomtopia today. 🚀

AI built for the way people actually work — in meetings, and far beyond. What excites me most: AI-enriched notes that extend your memory and productivity. They work seamlessly whether you’re in person, hybrid, or virtual — across Zoom, Teams, Meet, and Webex — powered by our Federated AI stack, delivering the industry’s highest quality transcription, summarization, and translation.

But that’s just the start.

✨ AI Companion is now an app — your personal hub for productivity and collaboration, either on the web or as the new home surface for Zoom Workplace. It helps you gain insights and take action across meetings, chat, email, calendar, and documents.

From scheduling to agenda-setting, prep to note-taking, recap to reporting, new agentic skills like deep research, writing assistance, and proactive notifications support the full meeting lifecycle. The Zoom way: higher quality, lower cost, and secure.

On our open platform, we’re also bringing AI Companion to where you work:
- Slack &amp; Teams: meeting channels with AI summaries and assets created automatically.
- Cross-platform readiness: AI Companion will assist you wherever you spend time including in Slack and Teams, while knowing your Google or Microsoft email, calendar and documents.
- Agent-to-Agent Protocol: orchestrating external agents (like ServiceNow) in AI Companion, and on other platforms including Google Agentspace and Salesforce Agentforce.

Bu sayede:

* Kitle etkileşimi ve içerik performansını,

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🚀 <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fzoomtopia&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Zoomtopia</a>’da büyük bir yenilik: <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Faicompanion&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AICompanion</a> 3.0!

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/zoom?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Zoom</a>, yalnızca toplantılarda değil; sohbet, e-posta, takvim ve belgeler genelinde de iş yapış şeklimizi dönüştürüyor.

En heyecan verici özelliklerden biri: <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fyapayzeka&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#yapayzeka</a> ile zenginleştirilmiş notlar. Artık hafızamızı ve verimliliğimizi genişleten bu güçlü özellik, Zoom’un Federated AI altyapısı sayesinde en yüksek kaliteli transkripsiyon, özetleme ve çeviri ile destekleniyor.

✨ Öne çıkanlar:
* AI Companion artık bir uygulama → Verimlilik ve işbirliği için kişisel merkez.
* Çapraz platform desteği → Google veya Microsoft e-posta, takvim ve belgelerinizi tanıyarak, Slack ve Teams dahil vakit geçirdiğiniz her yerde size yardımcı olacak.
* Yeni “Agent-to-Agent Protocol” → AI Companion içinde ServiceNow gibi harici ajanları ve Google Agentspace ile Salesforce Agentforce gibi diğer platformlardaki ajanları orkestre etme.
* Toplantı yaşam döngüsünün tamamında destek → Planlama, gündem, not alma, özet, raporlama, yazım desteği ve proaktif bildirimler.

Zoom tarzıyla: daha yüksek kalite, daha düşük maliyet, daha güvenli! 💡

👉 <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dm4iHedq?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dm4iHedq</a>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="feed-reshare-content__commentary">We launched AI Companion 3.0 at Zoomtopia today. 🚀

AI built for the way people actually work — in meetings, and far beyond. What excites me most: AI-enriched notes that extend your memory and productivity. They work seamlessly whether you’re in person, hybrid, or virtual — across Zoom, Teams, Meet, and Webex — powered by our Federated AI stack, delivering the industry’s highest quality transcription, summarization, and translation.

But that’s just the start.

✨ AI Companion is now an app — your personal hub for productivity and collaboration, either on the web or as the new home surface for Zoom Workplace. It helps you gain insights and take action across meetings, chat, email, calendar, and documents.

From scheduling to agenda-setting, prep to note-taking, recap to reporting, new agentic skills like deep research, writing assistance, and proactive notifications support the full meeting lifecycle. The Zoom way: higher quality, lower cost, and secure.

On our open platform, we’re also bringing AI Companion to where you work:
- Slack &amp; Teams: meeting channels with AI summaries and assets created automatically.
- Cross-platform readiness: AI Companion will assist you wherever you spend time including in Slack and Teams, while knowing your Google or Microsoft email, calendar and documents.
- Agent-to-Agent Protocol: orchestrating external agents (like ServiceNow) in AI Companion, and on other platforms including Google Agentspace and Salesforce Agentforce.

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="feed-reshare-content__commentary">🌐 Zoomtopia 2025 – Key Takeaways for the Future of AI &amp; Collaboration 

Couldn’t make it to Zoomtopia this year? No worries — the full recording is available, and it’s packed with groundbreaking announcements and insights. Watch the full session here
<a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/d2AhMFnU?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/d2AhMFnU</a>

📌 Smart Chapters &amp; Key Discussions:
 ⏱ 00:00 – Overcoming AI Implementation Challenges
 ⏱ 03:22 – Zoom's Custom AI Companion Strategy
 ⏱ 07:31 – Custom AI Companion in Action
 ⏱ 16:08 – Zoom RTMS (Real-Time Media Streams) Launch
 ⏱ 17:48 – RTMS in Action at Major League Baseball
 ⏱ 26:08 – AI-Driven Ecosystem Integration

🔍 What You’ll Learn:

⭐ Overcoming AI Barriers – Brendan Nittelson (Chief Ecosystem Officer, Zoom) outlined the biggest obstacles companies face in leveraging AI: fragmented tech stacks, siloed data, and lack of orchestration. Zoom’s open platform is positioned to connect workflows seamlessly across the enterprise.
 ⭐ Zoom’s Custom AI Companion Strategy – A flexible approach that allows customers to benefit from out-of-the-box AI features or build tailored solutions. With over 3,000 integrations, Zoom meets organizations where they are. ServiceNow is already on board with the first third-party AI Companion agent.
 ⭐ Real Use Case – Jeff Ritter, COO at Cumberland Mutual, explained how their team consolidated knowledge bases and AI tools within Zoom. The result: improved access to unstructured data, faster workflows, and plans to expand into Salesforce and policy-related tasks.
 ⭐ RTMS (Real-Time Media Streams) – One of the biggest announcements! Enterprises and developers now get direct access to Zoom’s media layer for building next-gen apps. Imagine specialized transcription, telehealth monitoring, compliance checks, and even AI-driven impersonation detection — all powered by Zoom RTMS.
 ⭐ Ecosystem Power – With more than 3,000 apps, Zoom integrates seamlessly with Microsoft, Google, Salesforce, and ServiceNow. This strengthens workflows and breaks down silos, enabling scalable AI-first operations.

🌟 Why It Matters:
Zoom is evolving far beyond video conferencing. With AI at its core, Zoom is building an ecosystem that empowers organizations to:
 ➡️ Streamline knowledge access and collaboration
 ➡️ Deploy real-time, AI-powered applications
 ➡️ Scale with open integrations and orchestration tools
 ➡️ Turn AI vision into practical enterprise workflows
💡 The future of collaboration is here — and it’s AI-driven, open, and deeply integrated.

At ETGi Grup, we are proud to be a Zoom EMEA Partner.
 We support organizations across the region with:
 ✨ Sales &amp; Licensing tailored to your needs
 ✨ End-to-End Support to ensure smooth adoption
 ✨ Training &amp; Enablement to help your teams unlock the full power of Zoom

👉 If you want to explore how Zoom’s AI-powered ecosystem can transform the way your organization works, we’re here to help.

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="feed-reshare-content__commentary">🌐 Zoomtopia 2025 – Key Takeaways for the Future of AI &amp; Collaboration 

Couldn’t make it to Zoomtopia this year? No worries — the full recording is available, and it’s packed with groundbreaking announcements and insights. Watch the full session here
<a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/d2AhMFnU?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/d2AhMFnU</a>

📌 Smart Chapters &amp; Key Discussions:
 ⏱ 00:00 – Overcoming AI Implementation Challenges
 ⏱ 03:22 – Zoom's Custom AI Companion Strategy
 ⏱ 07:31 – Custom AI Companion in Action
 ⏱ 16:08 – Zoom RTMS (Real-Time Media Streams) Launch
 ⏱ 17:48 – RTMS in Action at Major League Baseball
 ⏱ 26:08 – AI-Driven Ecosystem Integration

🔍 What You’ll Learn:

⭐ Overcoming AI Barriers – Brendan Nittelson (Chief Ecosystem Officer, Zoom) outlined the biggest obstacles companies face in leveraging AI: fragmented tech stacks, siloed data, and lack of orchestration. Zoom’s open platform is positioned to connect workflows seamlessly across the enterprise.
 ⭐ Zoom’s Custom AI Companion Strategy – A flexible approach that allows customers to benefit from out-of-the-box AI features or build tailored solutions. With over 3,000 integrations, Zoom meets organizations where they are. ServiceNow is already on board with the first third-party AI Companion agent.
 ⭐ Real Use Case – Jeff Ritter, COO at Cumberland Mutual, explained how their team consolidated knowledge bases and AI tools within Zoom. The result: improved access to unstructured data, faster workflows, and plans to expand into Salesforce and policy-related tasks.
 ⭐ RTMS (Real-Time Media Streams) – One of the biggest announcements! Enterprises and developers now get direct access to Zoom’s media layer for building next-gen apps. Imagine specialized transcription, telehealth monitoring, compliance checks, and even AI-driven impersonation detection — all powered by Zoom RTMS.
 ⭐ Ecosystem Power – With more than 3,000 apps, Zoom integrates seamlessly with Microsoft, Google, Salesforce, and ServiceNow. This strengthens workflows and breaks down silos, enabling scalable AI-first operations.

🌟 Why It Matters:
Zoom is evolving far beyond video conferencing. With AI at its core, Zoom is building an ecosystem that empowers organizations to:
 ➡️ Streamline knowledge access and collaboration
 ➡️ Deploy real-time, AI-powered applications
 ➡️ Scale with open integrations and orchestration tools
 ➡️ Turn AI vision into practical enterprise workflows
💡 The future of collaboration is here — and it’s AI-driven, open, and deeply integrated.

At ETGi Grup, we are proud to be a Zoom EMEA Partner.
 We support organizations across the region with:
 ✨ Sales &amp; Licensing tailored to your needs
 ✨ End-to-End Support to ensure smooth adoption
 ✨ Training &amp; Enablement to help your teams unlock the full power of Zoom

👉 If you want to explore how Zoom’s AI-powered ecosystem can transform the way your organization works, we’re here to help.
